[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA stack-based buffer overflow was detected in the `mg_json_get` function within the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mMongoose codebase. When processing a specially crafted input, the function writes [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mone byte past the end of its local `nesting` array. This issue was uncovered by a [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mLibFuzzer harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and reported by AddressSanitizer as a [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m-byte stack-buffer-overflow in `json.c` at line [0m[1;36m186[0m[39m.[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  During fuzz testing, `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` invokes `mg_json_get` with [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marbitrary data. AddressSanitizer reports a write beyond the bounds of a [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstack-allocated buffer named `nesting`:[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    • Overflowing write of size [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m at offset [0m[1;36m62[0m[39m in `mg_json_get`  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    • The `nesting` array is defined at line [0m[1;36m131[0m[39m of `src/mongoose/src/json.c` and [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mspans bytes [0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m32[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m62[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    • The overflow occurs at line [0m[1;36m186[0m[39m in `json.c`.[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  This is a classic stack-buffer-overflow vulnerability. A one-byte write exceeds [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe allocated stack space for the `nesting` array, potentially corrupting adjacent [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstack data.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key observations  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • AddressSanitizer log pinpoints the exact instruction and call stack:[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. `mg_json_get` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mjson.[0m[1;92mc:186[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtest/fuzz.[0m[1;92mc:81[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Fuzzer driver routines in LLVM’s libFuzzer.  [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The shadow-byte dump shows redzones around the `nesting` buffer, confirming a [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwrite into the redzone region.  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The fuzzer was run with [0m[1;36m100[0m[39m iterations under libFuzzer’s interactive mode, seed[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3941677225[0m[39m, and consistently reproduces the overflow.[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Code areas to investigate  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • `src/mongoose/src/json.c`, especially the definition and usage of the `nesting`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marray in `mg_json_get`.  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Logic in `mg_json_get` around JSON token traversal, boundary checks, and index [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcalculations that manipulate `nesting`.  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The fuzz harness in `src/mongoose/test/fuzz.c` [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m81[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m for context on [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhow inputs reach `mg_json_get`.[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA thorough review of those code regions will provide a holistic understanding of [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhy the overflow occurs and which control flows and inputs trigger it.[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Initial Issue Log[0m                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe initial issue is an AddressSanitizer–reported stack-buffer-overflow in the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunction `mg_json_get` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmongoose/src/json.[0m[1;92mc:186:28[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. A local array `nesting` was [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbeing indexed out of bounds. The patch attempt replaced the array declaration[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munsigned char nesting[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mMG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                                           [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhoping to increase its size. After rebuilding and rerunning the fuzzer for [0m[1;36m100[0m[39m [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39miterations, the same [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte write overflow at the same frame offset was reported [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39magain.[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Initial Issue  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - A libFuzzer run with AddressSanitizer triggered a stack-buffer-overflow in [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`mg_json_get`.  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The failing trace:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     #[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m  mg_json_get [0m[35m/src/mongoose/src/[0m[95mjson.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;92m186:28[0m                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - ASan reports the overflow occurs at offset [0m[1;36m62[0m[39m inside the `nesting` array, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhich spans bytes [0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m32[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m62[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m in the stack frame.  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The local variables in this frame include:[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     const char *s;[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     unsigned char nesting[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mMG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     int i, j, depth;[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` in test/fuzz.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m feeds arbitrary data [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minto `mg_json_get`, triggering the out-of-bounds write.[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Key Observations in the Initial Log  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The AddressSanitizer summary explicitly marks `nesting` as the overflow [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtarget.  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The overflow is a single-byte write, suggesting an index equals the array [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlength.  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The stack frame layout confirms `nesting` was allocated smaller than the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmaximum nesting depth encountered in the test input.  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch Attempt  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The patch changes the declaration at line [0m[1;36m127[0m[39m of `src/json.c`:[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```diff[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     +  unsigned char nesting[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mMG_JSON_MAX_NESTING[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No other code changes were made.  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The constants `MG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH` and `MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING` are presumably [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdefined elsewhere in the codebase.[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Post-Patch Log  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - A new fuzzer run [0m[1;39m([0m[39msame settings[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m immediately reproduces the same overflow:[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This indicates the size of `nesting` did not grow sufficiently [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor the wrong [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconstant was used[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, so the overflow persists.[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwith `unsigned char nesting[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mMG_JSON_MAX_NESTING[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` and inserted `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdepth >= [0m       [2m                [0m
